<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span style="text-decoration:underline"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>Corrupted Media Productions, Inc. – Privacy Policy</strong></span></span></p><p style="text-align:center;white-space:pre-wrap;" class=""><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><em>Updated 3/12/23</em></span></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Please read the following privacy policy carefully before using this software. Your use, distribution or installation of this software indicates your acceptance of this privacy policy.&nbsp; If you do not agree to any of the terms of this privacy policy, then do not install, distribute or use the software.&nbsp;</span></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Your privacy is important to Corrupted Media and we take our responsibility of caring for it seriously. This policy describes how Corrupted Media Productions Inc. ("Corrupted Media processes the personal information we may collect about you when you use our software products and services or when you attend live events hosted by or in connection with Corrupted Media (collectively, "Services"). In some cases, other subsidiaries and/or affiliates of Corrupted Media may be considered data controllers, either together with Corrupted Media or by themselves.&nbsp;</span></p><h2 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>1. Information We Collect</strong></span></h2><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br></span></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">The information we collect depends on what Services you use and how you use them. Please see below for more details.<br><br></span></p><ol data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>Information You Give Us Directly<br><br>We may collect information that you provide us, including but not limited to:</strong></span></p></li><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Your Corrupted Media Account information, including your email address, username, real name, country, date of birth, telephone number and password;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Security questions and answers;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Information you provide in response to surveys about our Services;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Information you provide when seeking help from us, such as your name, email address, records of the issues you experience; and</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Billing information, such as your name, payment card number, and payment account details.</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Images, including your avatar design choices.</span></p></li></ul></ol><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br></span></p><ol data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>Information You Provide When Playing Online<br><br>When you participate in social features such as chat, any audio, visual, and/or electronic information that you disclose may be read, copied, collected, or used by other players, and may become publicly available.&nbsp;</strong></span></p></li></ol><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br>When you participate in online multiplayer games, your in-game profile information, gameplay, and statistics are visible. We may record your gameplay in multi-player events and replay it to other players. In competitive game modes, we may record your gameplay, and your controller button inputs, and replay these together with your in-game profile information and game statistics to other players in-game and at live Corrupted Media or partner events.</span></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">We may collect information related to your virtual reality gaming environment, including but not limited to:</span></p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">How your physical body interacts with virtual reality, including your height, body movements, and arm span</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">The characteristics of how your physical environment interacts with virtual reality, including the measurements of any physical barriers in the room where you play our games</span></p></li></ul><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br></span></p><ol data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>Other Information We Collect When You Use Our Services<br><br>We may collect other information automatically when you use our Services, including but not limited to:</strong></span></p></li><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">IP address;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Information about your device, hardware, and software, such as your hardware identifiers, platform type, settings and components, Corrupted Media software and updates you have installed, and the presence of required plugins;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Approximate geolocation data (derived from IP or device settings);</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Details about what Corrupted Media games or Services you purchase or obtain, and your use of them;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Device event information, including crash reports, request and referral URLs and system activity details (e.g., whether you encountered an error playing our games or lost Internet access); and</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Other information (such as your likeness) that you may provide as part of your participation in live events.</span></p></li></ul></ol><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong><br></strong>We also may collect and store information locally on your device.</span></p><ol data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>Information Provided to Us by Third Parties<br><br>We may receive information about you contained in third-party user accounts when you use Corrupted Media online Services on or through third-party platforms. This information is provided to Corrupted Media as part of establishing or linking a Corrupted Media Account. Your use of Corrupted Media online Services through these third-parties indicates your agreement for the transfer of this information. These include, but are not limited to:&nbsp;</strong></span></p></li><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Playfab</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Photon</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Unity (includes Unity Analytics)</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Oculus</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Facebook</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Adverty</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Steam</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Paypal</span></p></li></ul></ol><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br></span></p><ol data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>Categories of Personal Information Processed<br><br>Depending on your use of our Services, the following categories of personal information may have been collected, shared, sold, or disclosed in the preceding 12 months (as these processing activities are defined under applicable privacy laws, such as the California Consumer Privacy Act “CCPA”):</strong></span></p></li><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Identifiers; such as a real name, user name, account name, email, online identifiers, device identifiers, IP address, or mobile device identifiers;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Purchase information; such as payment card number, payment account details, billing address , and other payment information;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Characteristics of Protected Classifications under state or federal law; such as age or gender;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Commercial Information; such as products or services interaction and purchase history;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Internet or Electronic Network Activity information; such as browsing history, search history, and information regarding interactions with our games, websites, applications, and/or advertisements;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Approximate (coarse) geolocation data; such as location data derived from IP address or device settings;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Audio or Electronic information; such as when you play our games, play certain multiplayer modes, use chat features, or participate in competitive game modes or live events;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Inferences; such as consumer preferences drawn from the above.</span></p></li></ul></ol><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong><br></strong>In certain situations we may collect additional information, for example:</span></p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">If you are the recipient of a contest or prize that requires tax reporting, we may collect identifiers associated with your government-issued documents (such as a social security number).</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">If you participate in our competitive gaming events, we may collect identifiers associated with your government-issued documents (such as a passport number), financial information (such as bank accounts), and health-related information.</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">If you participate in our user experience research, we may collect financial information (such as bank accounts), health-related information and video footage of your gameplay, as well as your recorded image throughout the session.<br><br><br></span></p></li></ul><h2 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>2. How We Collect Information</strong></span></h2><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br></span></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">We and third parties may use technologies described below to collect information to deliver our Services.<br><br></span></p><ol data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>Cookies and Similar Technologies<br><br>Cookies are small text files stored on your Internet browser. We and our third-party partners may use cookies and similar tracking technologies to help us understand things like what web pages, features, or ads you view and what games you play. You can disable cookies, limit the types of cookies you allow, or set your browser to alert you when cookies are being sent. Please refer to guidance provided by your individual web browser if you'd like help in managing your cookie preferences. We also offer cookie consent tools in certain regions to help you manage your cookies.<br><br>We may use tracking pixels or clear GIFs to collect information about your use of our Services and your response to our marketing emails. We use Internet log files (which contain technical data such as your IP address) to monitor traffic on our Services, troubleshoot technical problems, detect and prevent fraud, and enforce our End User License Agreement. <br><br>We also may use Analytics, Advertising, Anti-Cheat, and Anti-Fraud technologies in our Services. These technologies may utilize the same cookies or similar mechanisms as further described below.</strong></span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>Analytics Technologies<br><br>We may use internal and third-party analytics technologies to collect information about how you use our Services, your computer or device and the health of our Services.<br><br>For instance, we may collect and store data from your computer or device when you use our Services. This information includes technical and related information about your computer or device and operating and/or network systems (such as IP Address and device ID), information about your engagement with certain features, gameplay and usage statistics, system interactions and hardware. If you play a game offline without connecting to the Internet, this data may be stored on your device and transmitted to us when your device connects to the Internet. If you participate in online Services, we may also collect, use, store, transmit and publicly display your personal and/or statistical data regarding your game play (including scores, rankings and achievements), or identify content that is created and shared by you with other players.<br><br>Third-party analytics technologies integrated into our Services may (including SDK [Software Development Kit] and API [Application Program Interfaces] integrations) combine the information they collect in connection with your use of Corrupted Media's Services with information they have independently collected over time and/or across different platforms. Many of these companies collect and use information pursuant to their own privacy policies.&nbsp;</strong></span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>Ad Serving Technologies<br><br>Some of our Services may employ ad serving technologies that use cookies, clear GIFs, web beacons, tracking pixels, SDK, API, and other similar technologies to deliver offers and advertising to you within Corrupted Media Services as well as on third-party platforms and sites, and to measure the performance of our advertising campaigns. Some of these technologies can sync or connect behaviour across different websites and devices to tailor offers and advertising to your interests. For instance, you may be presented with an offer for a game we think you might enjoy. Or, if you express interest in a game, you may receive an advertisement later for that game or similar Services on Corrupted Media or third-party sites. Other in-game advertising technologies enable offers to be temporarily uploaded to your game, web browser, or mobile device and later replaced while you are online.<br><br>These technologies collect and use information so we can serve appropriate offers and advertising to you, to measure effectiveness and distribution of these offers and advertising, and to understand how users interact with our Services. In addition to identifiers and certain information listed above, this information may include:</strong></span></p></li><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Advertisements served and the location of the ad;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Length of time an advertisement was visible;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Domain type, IP address, size of the advertisement;</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Your interaction, if any, with the ad; and</span></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Advertisement response.</span></p></li></ul></ol><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Third-party advertising companies may combine the information collected in the context of delivering an offer to you via our Services with other information they have independently collected over time and/or across different websites. Many of these companies collect and use information pursuant to their own privacy policies.&nbsp;</span></p><ol data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>Anti-Cheat and Fraud Prevention Technologies<br><br>When you use our Services, we or third parties may use cookies and similar technologies and collect data about your machine or device, to create a machine "fingerprint" or "hash" of your machine components, for fraud prevention, security and authentication purposes. We may also monitor publicly-available information, third-party sites, and/or use anti-cheat technology within our Services, including automated anti-fraud and abuse algorithms.</strong></span></p></li></ol><h2 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>3. We require that any third party use the data only on our behalf and for purposes consistent with this policy.<br><br><strong>Business partners.</strong>&nbsp;We may provide personal information to business partners with whom we jointly offer Services. These partners include the companies that provide the platform on which you play our games.<br><br><strong>Affiliates.</strong>&nbsp;We may share personal information with our affiliated companies as is necessary for the purposes outlined in this notice.<br><br><strong>Advertising partners.&nbsp;</strong>Through our Services, we may allow third-party advertising partners to utilize technologies and other tracking tools to collect information regarding your use of Corrupted Media's Services and your device (e.g., your IP address, mobile identifiers, page(s) visited, location, browser information, time of day). We may also combine and share such information and other information (such as your de-identified account information, demographic information, hardware specifications, and past purchase history) with third-party advertising partners. These advertising partners may use this information (and similar information collected from other websites) for purposes of delivering targeted advertisements to you when you visit third-party websites within their networks. This practice is commonly referred to as "interest-based advertising" or "online behavioural advertising." We may allow access to other data collected by the Services to share information that may be useful, relevant, valuable, or otherwise of interest to you.<br><br><strong>Disclosures to protect us or others.&nbsp;</strong>We may access, preserve, and disclose any information we store associated with you to external parties if we, in good faith, believe doing so is required or appropriate to: comply with law enforcement or national security requests and legal process, such as a court order or subpoena; protect your, our or others' rights, property, or safety; enforce our policies or contracts; collect amounts owed to us; or assist with an investigation or prosecution of suspected or actual illegal activity.&nbsp;</span></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br><strong>Disclosure in the event of merger, sale, or other asset transfer.</strong>&nbsp;In the event of a reorganization, divestiture, merger, sale, or bankruptcy, we may transfer all information we collect to the relevant third party and will obtain your consent to do so if required by law or contract.<br><br><strong>Third-party plugins.</strong>&nbsp;When third-party technologies or social tools are integrated into our Services, those third parties may collect information about your use of our Services.&nbsp;</span></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br><strong>Cross-Platform Sharing.</strong>&nbsp;Some of our games may allow you to connect and play with friends and members of a game's community, regardless of what platform they play on. That other platform may receive your platform's information to facilitate game interaction. We will share your information with platforms to the extent necessary to enable gaming features. Your information received by these platforms may be subject to their respective privacy notices.<br><br><strong>With Your Consent.</strong>&nbsp;We may share information with other third parties with your express consent, unless otherwise described above. For example, you may agree to us sharing your information with a certain company or organization to hear about their products, services, or promotions, or if you tell us that you want to link your Corrupted Media Account with another company’s services. Use of the information you agree to share will be subject to those third parties' respective privacy notices.<br><br></span></p><h2 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>5. Where We Hold Your Information</strong></span></h2><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br></span></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Personal information we collect may be stored and processed for the purposes set out in this Privacy and Cookie Policy in the United States or any other country in which Corrupted Media, its subsidiaries, or third-party agents operate. By consenting to the transfer of your personal data outside of your country of residence, you acknowledge that your personal information may be transferred to recipients in the United States and other countries that may not offer the same level of privacy protection as the laws in your country of residence or citizenship.<br><br></span></p><h2 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>6. How We Protect Your Information</strong></span></h2><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br></span></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Security of your information is a priority at Corrupted Media. Even so, please be aware that no security measure is 100% perfect. Thus we cannot guarantee the security of your information at all times. You should always be diligent when it comes to the protection of your personal information.<br><br></span></p><h2 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>7. Children</strong></span></h2><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br></span></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Corrupted Media recognizes the importance of protecting children's privacy online. As applicable, we strive to follow the different minimum age guidelines set by the laws of individual countries or territories when determining the age that children can access certain features of our Services.<br><br>Our products in production have a click box upon registration where users must identify themselves as being at least 13 years old.&nbsp; People under age 13 will not be allowed to register.</span></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br>We encourage you to talk with your children about communicating with strangers and the risks of disclosing personal information online. <br><br></span></p><h2 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>8. Your Choices and Controls</strong></span></h2><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br>Please contact us if you have a concern about your privacy.&nbsp; We will work with you to address it. If you are looking to have all information collected for your account deleted from our database, reach out to us at verticalshiftgame@gmail.com.<br><br></span></p><h2 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>9. Third-Party Services</strong></span></h2><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><br></span></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent">Our websites and Services may contain advertising or links to third-party services. If you visit a third-party website or use a third-party service, you should consult that service's or site's privacy policy as your use of third-party sites or services is governed by their privacy policies.<br><br></span></p><h2 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--lightAccent"><strong>10.
